CMS Chronic Conditions Warehouse (CCW) Data Dictionary
Assessment — Minimum Data Set (MDS) File
Version —  April 2026
Variable sequence	Short SAS name	Long SAS name	Label	Type	Length	Description	Codes	Comments
1	BENE_ID	BENE_ID	Encrypted 723 Beneficiary ID	CHAR	15	A unique CCW beneficiary identifier field that is specific to the Chronic Condition Warehouse.  This field is encrypted prior to delivery to researchers. The BENE_ID field is used to cross-reference data for each beneficiary across all claim and assessment data files.		Not in CMS extract
2	ASMT_ID	ASMT_ID	Encrypted Assessment ID	CHAR	15	This number is assigned when an assessment record is processed in the Chronic Condition Warehouse.  This field is encrypted prior to delivery to researchers.  It identifies lines that are submitted from the same assessment.
3	TRGT_DT	TRGT_DT	Target Date (Date of Assessment)	DATE	8	For MDS, the target date is the A2000 Discharge Date for any discharge, the A1600 Reentry Date for any re-entry and the A2300 Assessment Reference Date for any other type of assessment.  For SB the Target Date is the same as the Event Date and is equal to the following dates: 10a (A2300) - Assessment Reference Date, 15 (A2000) - Discharge Date and 16 (A1600) - Reentry Date.
4	STATE_CD	STATE_CD	State Code	CHAR	2	This column contains the two-digit state abbreviation code.	AK=Alaska
AL=Alabama
AP=APO
AR=Arkansas
AS=American Samoa
AZ=Arizona
CA=California
CN=Canada
CO=Colorado
CT=Connecticut
DC=District of Columbia
DE=Delaware
FL=Florida
FM=Micronesia
FN=Foreign
GA=Georgia
GU=Guam
HI=Hawaii
IA=Iowa
ID=Idaho
IL=Illinois
IN=Indiana
KS=Kansas
KY=Kentucky
LA=Louisiana
MA=Massachusetts
MD=Maryland
ME=Maine
MH=Marshall Islands
MI=Michigan
MN=Minnesota
MO=Missouri
MP=Saipan/Mariana Is.
MS=Mississippi
MT=Montana
MX=Mexico
NC=North Carolina
ND=North Dakota
NE=Nebraska
NH=New Hampshire
NJ=New Jersey
NM=New Mexico
NV=Nevada
NY=New York
OH=Ohio
OK=Oklahoma

PA=Pennsylvania

WV=West Virginia
WY=Wyoming
5	FAC_PRVDR_INTRNL_ID	Facility/Provider Internal ID	Facility/Provider Internal ID	NUM	12	This column contains the facility internal ID for nursing home facilities or the provider internal number for swing bed providers.
6	MDS_ASMT_ID	MDS_ASMT_ID	Encrypted MDS Assessment Internal ID	NUM	12	Unique identifier for a version of an assessment when combined with State ID.
7	MDS_ITM_SBST_CD	MDS_ITM_SBST_CD	Item Subset Code (ISC)	CHAR	4	This column contains the item subset code and identifies the type of assessment that was submitted. This code is derived from the values submitted in A0310A, A0310B, A0310C, A0310D and A0310F in conjunction with the value submitted in A0200 - type of provider.	NC=Nursing Home: Comprehensive
ND=Nursing Home: Discharge
NO=Nursing Home: OMRA Other
NOD=Nursing Home: OMRA Other + Discharge
NP=Nursing Home: PPS
NQ=Nursing Home: Quarterly
NS=Nursing Home: OMRA Start of Therapy
NSD=Nursing Home: OMRA Start of Therapy + Discharge
NT=Nursing Home: Tracking (entry/expired)
SD=Swing Bed: Discharge
SO=Swing Bed: OMRA Other
SP=Swing Bed: PPS
SS=Swing Bed: OMRA Start of Therapy
SSD=Swing Bed: OMRA Start of Therapy + Discharge
ST=Swing Bed: Tracking (entry/expired)
XX=Inactivation
8	SUBMSN_DT	SUBMSN_DT	Submission Date	DATE	8	This column contains the date the submission file was received by the system.
9	MDS_CRCTN_STUS_CD	MDS_CRCTN_STUS_CD	Correction Status Code	CHAR	1	This column contains the correction status code indicating the status of the assessment: current (C), modified (M) or inactivated (X).	C=Current Assessment
I=Inactivation Requested
M=Modified by a Subsequent Submission
X=Inactivated by a Subsequent Submission
10	ORGNL_ASMT_ID	ORGNL_ASMT_ID	Encrypted Original Assessment ID	NUM	15	This column contains the unique ID of the assessment where the Correction Number is equal to '00'.
11	V0100F_PRIOR_STF_MOOD_SCRE_NUM	V0100F_PRIOR_STF_MOOD_SCRE_NUM	Prior Assessment Staff Assessment of Resident Mood (PHQ-9) Total Severity Score Number	CHAR	2	Prior Assessment Staff Assessment of Resident Mood (PHQ-9) Total Severity Score Number
12	C_RSDNT_AGE_NUM	C_RSDNT_AGE_NUM	Resident Age	CHAR	8	This column contains the system calculated resident age number.
13	C_URBN_RRL_CD	C_URBN_RRL_CD	CBSA Urban/Rural Code	CHAR	1	This data in this column identifies whether the facility is designated to be in a rural or urban area.
14	C_MDCR_HIPPS_TXT	C_MDCR_HIPPS_TXT	Recalculated Z0100A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare Part A HIPPS code.
15	C_MDCR_RUG_VRSN_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG_VRSN_TXT	Recalculated Z0100B	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare Part A RUG version code.
16	C_MDCR_STAY_CD	C_MDCR_STAY_CD	Recalculated Z0100C	CHAR	1	The data in this column is an output value that is produced by the grouper and indicates whether the short-stay logic was used to calculate the RUG.		discontinued 09/30/2023
17	C_MDCR_SET_CD	C_MDCR_SET_CD	CMI Set for Recalculated Z0100A	CHAR	3	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare Set Code used for the Part A RUG.		discontinued 09/30/2023
18	C_MDCR_CMI_TXT	C_MDCR_CMI_TXT	CMI Value for Recalculated Z0100A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare CMI value returned for the Part A RUG.		discontinued 09/30/2023
19	C_MDCR_NT_HIPPS_TXT	C_MDCR_NT_HIPPS_TXT	Recalculated Z0150A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare non-therapy Part A HIPPS code.		discontinued 09/30/2023
20	C_MDCR_NT_RUG_VRSN_TXT	C_MDCR_NT_RUG_VRSN_TXT	Recalculated Z0150B	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare non-therapy RUG version code.		discontinued 09/30/2023
21	C_MDCR_NT_SET_CD	C_MDCR_NT_SET_CD	CMI Set for Recalculated Z0150A	CHAR	3	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare non-therapy Set Code.		discontinued 09/30/2023
22	C_MDCR_NT_CMI_TXT	C_MDCR_NT_CMI_TXT	CMI Value for Recalculated Z0150A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the calculated Medicare non-therapy CMI value.		discontinued 09/30/2023
23	C_STATE_RUG_GRP_TXT	C_STATE_RUG_GRP_TXT	Recalculated Z0200A	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the calculated state Medicaid RUG case mix group code.
24	C_STATE_RUG_VRSN_TXT	C_STATE_RUG_VRSN_TXT	Recalculated Z0200B	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the calculated state Medicaid RUG version code.
25	C_STATE_SET_CD	C_STATE_SET_CD	CMI Set for Recalculated Z0200A	CHAR	3	The data in this column contains the calculated state Medicaid RUG Set Code.
26	C_STATE_CMI_TXT	C_STATE_CMI_TXT	CMI Value for Recalculated Z0200A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the calculated state Medicaid CMI text.
27	C_STATE_2_RUG_GRP_TXT	C_STATE_2_RUG_GRP_TXT	Recalculated Z0250A	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the second calculated state Medicaid RUG case mix group code.
28	C_STATE_2_RUG_VRSN_TXT	C_STATE_2_RUG_VRSN_TXT	Recalculated Z0250B	CHAR	10	The data in this column contains the second calculated state Medicaid RUG version code.
29	C_STATE_2_SET_CD	C_STATE_2_SET_CD	CMI Set for Recalculated Z0250A	CHAR	3	The data in this column contains the second calculated state Medicaid RUG Set Code.
30	C_STATE_2_CMI_TXT	C_STATE_2_CMI_TXT	CMI Value for Recalculated Z0250A	CHAR	7	The data in this column contains the second calculated state Medicaid CMI text.
31	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_GRP_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_GRP_TXT	Medicare RUG III Index Maximized Group	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG III Medicare Index Maximized Group code.
32	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_VRSN_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_VRSN_TXT	Medicare RUG III Index Maximized Version	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG III Medicare Index Maximized Version text.
33	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_CMI_SET_CD	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_CMI_SET_CD	Medicare RUG III Index Maximized CMI Set	CHAR	3	This column contains the calculated RUG III Medicare Index Maximized Case Mix Index text.
34	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_CMI_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG3_IDX_MAX_CMI_TXT	Medicare RUG III Index Maximized CMI Value	CHAR	7	This column contains the calculated RUG III Medicare Index Maximized Case Mix Index Set Code.
35	C_MDCR_RUG3_HIRCHCL_GRP_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG3_HIRCHCL_GRP_TXT	Medicare RUG III Hierarchical Group	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG III Hierarchical Medicare RUG Group code.
36	C_MDCR_RUG3_HIRCHCL_VRSN_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG3_HIRCHCL_VRSN_TXT	Medicare RUG III Hierarchical Version	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG III Hierarchical Medicare RUG Group Version code.
37	C_MDCR_RUG4_HIRCHCL_GRP_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG4_HIRCHCL_GRP_TXT	Medicare RUG IV Hierarchical Group	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG IV Hierarchical Medicare RUG Group code.
38	C_MDCR_RUG4_HIRCHCL_VRSN_TXT	C_MDCR_RUG4_HIRCHCL_VRSN_TXT	Medicare RUG IV Hierarchical Version	CHAR	10	This column contains the calculated RUG IV Hierarchical Medicare RUG Group Version code.
39	A0050_TRANS_TYPE_CD	A0050_TRANS_TYPE_CD	A0050 Type of Record Code	CHAR	1	This column identifies the type of record submitted.	1=Add a new record
2= Modify existing record
3=Inactivate existing record
^=Blank(skip pattern)	effective 4/01/2012
40	A0100A_NPI_NUM	A0100A_NPI_NUM	A0100A Facility National Provider Identifier (NPI)	CHAR	10	This column contains the facility or provider's National Provider Identifier number.
41	A0100B_CMS_CRTFCTN_NUM	A0100B_CMS_CRTFCTN_NUM	A0100B Facility CMS Certification Number (CCN)	CHAR	12	This column contains the facility or provider's CMS Certification (Medicare) Number.
42	A0100C_STATE_PRVDR_NUM	A0100C_STATE_PRVDR_NUM	A0100C State Provider Number	CHAR	15	This column contains the facility or provider's state-assigned provider number.
43	A0200_PRVDR_TYPE_CD	A0200_PRVDR_TYPE_CD	A0200 Type of Provider	CHAR	1	This column identifies the type of provider (nursing home or swing bed) submitting the assessment. This value is used in conjunction with the Type of Assessment fields (A0310A, A0310B, A0310C, A0310D and A0310F) to determine the ISC.	1=Nursing home (SNF/NF)
2=Swing bed
44	A0310A_FED_OBRA_CD	A0310A_FED_OBRA_CD	A0310A Federal OBRA Reason for Assessment Code	CHAR	2	This column contains the federal OBRA reason for assessment value.	01=Admission assessment (required by day 14)
02=Quarterly review assessment
03=Annual assessment
04=Significant change in status assessment
05=Significant correction to prior comprehensive assessment
06=Significant correction to prior quarterly assessment
99=None of the above
45	A0310B_PPS_CD	A0310B_PPS_CD	A0310B PPS Assessment Code	CHAR	2	This column contains the PPS (Prospective Payment System) reason for assessment value.	01=5-day scheduled assessment
02=14-day scheduled assessment
03=30-day scheduled assessment
04=60-day scheduled assessment
05=90-day scheduled assessment
06=Readmission/return assessment
07=Unscheduled assessment used for PPS (OMRA, significant or clinical change, or significant correction assessment)
08=IPA - Interim Payment Assessment
99=None of the above
46	A0310C_PPS_OMRA_CD	A0310C_PPS_OMRA_CD	A0310C PPS Other Medicare Required Assessment (OMRA) Code	CHAR	1	This column contains the PPS Other Medicare Required Assessment value.	0=No
1=Start of therapy assessment
2=End of therapy assessment
3=Both Start and End of therapy assessment
4 = Change of therapy assessment	discontinued 9/30/2019
47	A0310D_SB_CLNCL_CHG_CD	A0310D_SB_CLNCL_CHG_CD	A0310D Swing Bed Clinical Change Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column indicates if the assessment is a swing bed clinical change assessment.	0=No
1=Yes
^=Blank (Skip Pattern)	discontinued 9/30/2019
48	A0310E_FIRST_SINCE_ADMSN_CD	A0310E_FIRST_SINCE_ADMSN_CD	A0310E First Assessment Since Most Recent Admission Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column indicates if this assessment is the first assessment since the most recent admission.	0=No
1=Yes
49	A0310F_ENTRY_DSCHRG_CD	A0310F_ENTRY_DSCHRG_CD	A0310F Entry/Discharge Code	CHAR	2	The data in this column indicates whether the assessment is an Entry or Discharge record.	01=Entry tracking record
10=Discharge assessment - return not anticipated
11=Discharge assessment - return anticipated
12=Death in facility record tracking record
99=None of the above
50	A0310G_PLND_DSCHRG_CD	A0310G_PLND_DSCHRG_CD	A0310G Planned Discharge Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column indicates the type of discharge code.	1 = Planned
2 = Unplanned
^ = Blank (skip pattern)	effective 10/01/2012
51	A0410_RQRD_SUBMSN_CD	A0410_RQRD_SUBMSN_CD	A0410 Submission Required Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column indicates if the assessment is a SUB_REQ (submission required) 2 [State Required] or 3 [Federal Required] submission.	1=Neither federal nor state required submission
2=State but not federal required submission (FOR NURSING HOMES ONLY)
3=Federal required submission

87	B0200_HEARG_CD	B0200_HEARG_CD	B0200 Hearing Code	CHAR	1	This data in this column identifies the resident's ability to hear.	-=Not assessed/no information
0=Adequate-no difficulty in normal conversation, social interaction,
listening to TV
1=Minimal difficulty-difficulty in some environments (e.g.,when person
speaks softly or setting is noisy
2=Moderate difficulty-speaker has to increase volume and speak distinctly
3=High impaired-absence of useful hearing
^=Blank(skip pattern)

90	B0700_SELF_UNDRSTOD_CD	B0700_SELF_UNDRSTOD_CD	B0700 Makes Self Understood Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column identifies the resident's ability to make themselves understood.	-=Not assessed/no information
0=Understood
1=Usually understood-difficulty communicating some words or finishing

2=Sometimes understood-ability is limited to making concrete requests

91	B0800_UNDRST_OTHR_CD	B0800_UNDRST_OTHR_CD	B0800 Ability to Understand Others Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column identifies the resident's ability to understand others.	-=Not assessed/no information

2=Sometimes understands-responds adequately to simple, direct

218	G0110F2_LOCOMTN_OFF_SPRT_CD	G0110F2_LOCOMTN_OFF_SPRT_CD	G0100F2 ADL Assistance: Locomotion Off Support Provided Code	CHAR	1	The data in this column identifies the resident's self-performance ability for locomotion off support provided.	-=Not assessed/no information

  1=Epithelial tissue-new skin growing in superficial ulcer. It can be light   pink and shiny, even in persons with pigmented skin.
